1. Find the item(s) you want to buy in the catalog.
2. Paste or type the entire wanted item listing(s) into an email to cmxmusic@gmail.com
   Include what you want for shipping method, payment method and insurance.
3. CMX will email you back telling you the items are being held (if available)
   and the total.
4. Send payment via PayPal, check, money order, etc. and address.
5. If shipping to or paying from outside USA please email cmxmusic@gmail.com

If you have questions, feel free to send an email cmxmusic@gmail.com

[- Please keep in mind that these are sometimes only best guesses -]

[!]=2 Titles On 1 Disc   [A]=Autographed           [Ax3]=3 Autographs
[B]=Best Of Collection   [C]=Cardboard Case        [D]=Front Insert Damage
[E]=Extra/Bonus Tracks   [Ex3]=3 Extra/BonusTracks [H]=HDCD(High Definition)
[I]=Front Insert Missing [J]=IncludesJapaneseLyrcs [K]=Plastic Sleeve
[M]=Marks On CD Front    [N]=No Back Insert        [O]=Promo/Advance Release
[P]=Plastic&CardbrdCase  [Q]=Case Damage           [R]=CDROM-Data
[S]=Reissue              [T]=CD Thincase           [U]=Unopened/StillSealed
[Z]=Scratched,Plays Fine

s/t=Self-Titled
orig=original issue (not a reissue)
{x}=contains {x} number of versions of the song


Listings include format(C=CD,T=Tape,V=Video,etc), artist/band, music styles,
title, year(if there's enough room), codes if any(U=unopened,S=reissue,etc),
record label(if there's enough room), and price. If there's any extra infor-
mation it's usually at the end:

FORMAT Artist(STYLE)Title YEAR [codes if any] Label...$PRICE possible extra info

All items are used & undamaged* full length regular issue (not accompanyment
tracks, EPs, etc)in regular cases with front & back inserts unless otherwise
listed.  None are CDR copies unless specifically listed as such.  All prices
are in US Dollars.  *Used items may possibly have VERY  minor scratches, etc
(that do not affect play at all).  If you only want ABSOLUTLY perfect items,
please order only items listed as "[U]" for unopened.
